 People meet in different parts of the world in many different ways
 inamen haath milaane lekar gale milane, tali bajaane or yahaan tak ki flying kis karnaa tak shaamil he
 Learn about such ways of greeting in different countries that will surprise you
 
 
 1
 Tawalu: If you want to live in this beautiful country, situated on the sea side, you have to smell
 tuvaalu main mehmaan ke swaagat main kiye jane vaale abhivadan ko sogi kehete hai
 In this, the welcoming person takes a deep breath and feels the fragrance by pressing the guest's face
 2
 Kenya: It has the longest reception greetings compared to the rest of the world
 kenya kaa maasai adivasee samudaay ke log apane mehmaan ke swaagat main adamu nrity karte hai
 a dance is heard there before the dance and then sprung into the circle
 isamen sabase sabhi kii koshish oonche se ooncha kudane kii hoti he
 Such a reception is rarely held in any other corner of the world
 3
 New Zealand: In New Zealand, a ritual called h होंगीngi is played during the reception under Maori tradition
 isamen jab do log aapas main milte hai to naak ko choote or ragadate hai
 They also associate this welcome way with the breath of life
 4
 Greenland / Lapland: Eskimo living in very cold people welcome each other lightly by rubbing their noses
 ise kunik kaha jaataa he
 Apart from this, during the meeting, people try to identify the hair and cheek of the guest
 aise wo nae logon ko unke andaaj se pahchaanane kii koshish karte hai
 Tibet: Seeing someone tongue out is undoubtedly considered bad in us or in many other countries
 lekin tibet main kuch is tareeke se aap milte samay mehmaan kaa abhivadan yaa swaagat karte hai
 This practice has been going on since the era of cruel Langdrama, the Tibetan king of Kali Juban who ruled in the 9th century
 darasal milanevaale ko jeebh dikhaakar tibeti log yah bataate hai ki raja langaderma se unka koi sambandh nahin he or na hi unki jeebh kaali he
